@## / /
mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos sna tshogs gsal ba zhes pa ming gzhan mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs // @# / /
rgya gar skad du /
a b+hi d+hA na shA s+t+ra bi shwa lo tsa na mi t+ya sa rA b+hi d+hA na mu k+t+ya ba lI nA ma /
bod skad du /
mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos sna tshogs gsal rab zhes pa ming gzhan mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba /
bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo / /
bcom ldan 'das dang de'i chos rgyal bar gyur cig dbyangs can rab tu dang bar mdzod / /
skye 'gro rnams la bde ba 'byung zhing dregs dang mi dge ba las drang bar mdzod / /
bdag gis gang zhig legs par sbyar ba'i bum pa mchog las byung ba'i chu 'dir yang / /
ci zhes lhags par byed pa don la mkhas pa rnams kyis kun tu 'jug par mdzod /
1 /
sde tshan don du mtha' dag snying stobs la dad dpal / /
dpal ldan snyan ngag mkhan po thub pa'i sde zhes byung / /
bdag gi rig pa'i gnas ni tshig ldan ngag snyan bcas / /
grags ldan bstan bcos mtha' dag las ni rjes su bsdus /
2 /
de phyir ngag gi rang bzhin ma lus pha rol gzigs gyur pa / /
sa gzhi la gnas 'dren pa rnams kyi yid brtan snod du gyur / /
dpal ldan dpal 'dzin gyis ni snyan ngag mkhan mchog mtha' dag gis / /
sbyar ba'i de nyid bdud rtsi'i btung ba 'chi med dbyangs can ldan /
3 /
de ni phul byung snyan ngag mkhan gyi lam skyes brling ba can / /
blo yi mig ldan bla mas bstan pa'i mig dang ldan pa yis / /
sna tshogs snyan ngag mkhan dbang gis bkod mngon brjod mdzad rnams las / /
drangs te mig dang 'dra ba 'di ni sgron me'i mdzod lta bu / /
rtog ge dang bcas snyan ngag mkhan gyi lung skyes brling ba rnams / /
kun tu snang byas rig gnas rnams kyi grong du nges gnas shing / /
spobs pa ldan pa rnams kyi blo yi lam dang 'dres byas pas / /
da ni 'di yis skye ngan rnams kyi tshig kyang bcom par 'gyur /
5 /
'bad pas dal bar gyur dang ma gyur ma lus rig pa dang / /
rig pa 'dzin pa stobs ldan rnams kyi blo la nges sbyar ba / /
dri med rin chen kaustu b+ha 'dir slar yang rlom dor nas / /
dpal mo'i dpal yon bzhin du rgya chen kho lag mchis 'di la'o /
6 /
klu yi dbang po yang dag gnas pa'i mdzod gyur rgya mtsho'i dbus / /
sna tshogs snyan ngag mkhan dbang kha yi nya phyis las byung ba / /
mkhas pa 'chi med kyis sprul dar gyi srad bu la brgyus nas / /
mu tig phreng ba bkod 'di snying la yang dag gzhag par mdzod /
7 /
'dod chags bral ba'i dri bzangs kyi / /
snyan grags me tog ra ba ni / /
bsten las 'di yi zhabs gnas pa / /
gang yang klu shing lta bur lhags /
8 /
gang zhig sgra la mkhas pa rnams dang mngon brjod 'dzin pa rnams dang 'jig rten pa / /
de dag gis kyang deng nyid mthong na yid la dga' ba lhag par skyed par byed / /
des na bdag gis 'bad pa 'di de lhag par gzhan gyi ched du bstan par 'gyur / /
bdag gis rgol ba rnams ni dga' ba'i ched du dregs pa 'joms byed byas par gyur /
9 /
dang por mang du mkhyen rnams kyis / /
sgra la 'bras bu gang bzhed pa / /
de 'dir 'chi med lugs rnams kyis / /
bdag gis sgra rnams nges par dgod /
10 /
mtho ris mi zad gnas bzang dang / /
gzhi gsum pa dang /
gnam dang /
mkha' / /

chu skyes rig 'dzin mi 'am ci / /
dri za gsang ba pa sha za / /
gnod sbyin srin po 'byung po dang / /
grub pa 'di rnams lha las byung / /
r-i zhes bya ba dang mi sbyin ma / /
lha yi ma'o sngon skyes pa / /
zla ba'i sbugs gnas mtshon cha bkod / /
bdud rtsi zas dang mtshun gyi ni / /
gzhon nu la sogs de rnams kyang / /
sbyin skyes dang ni mchod sbyin dgra / /
sngon gyi lha dang sbyin ma'i bu / /
sbyin skyes dbang po'i dgra sbyin byung / /
pa sangs slob ma sa 'og gnas / /

kai ke ya dang ku tsa dang / /

de rnams so /
15 /
sbyin ma sbyin skyes ma dang ni / /
sbyin skyes skyong ma di ti'o / /
sangs rgyas la mtshan bdun cu rtsa gnyis /
4 /
kun mkhyen bde gshegs ston pa dang / /
gnyis med gsung ba de bzhin gshegs / /
kun tu bzang po rdzogs sangs rgyas / /
thub pa sangs rgyas thub pa che / /
dpal stug thugs rje mdzad pa dang / /
bdud 'dul rgyal ba 'jig rten 'dul / /
skyob pa thub dbang bcom ldan 'das / /
mngon shes drug ldan rnam par 'dren / /
byams pa'i stobs mnga' stobs bcu mnga' / /
sa bcu'i dbang phyug rgyal ba dang / /
mchod 'os bcu pa spyan bcu gnyis / /
thams cad gzigs pa stobs chen ldan / /
chags bral skyabs gsum sku gsum pa / /
'og min bzhugs dang chags 'joms dang / /
chos kyi rgyal po mun pa 'joms / /
mkha' mnyam pa dang mi mnyam pa / /
rtogs ldan yon tan 'byung gnas dang / /
rnam shes tsam pa mkhyen lnga pa / /
ma hA ba la /
chos sku chos dbyings chos tri mu tri /
'khor ba / /
shin tu nges pa bde chen pa / /
stobs chen sems chen stobs chen pa / /
rgyal ba'i dbang po 'ba' zhig pa / /
rdo rje can dang yang dag sbas / /
dgra bcom pa dang bzod mang ba / /
'jig rten mgon po dus gsum mkhyen / /
pha rol phyin bcu 'chang ba dang / /
nam mkha' mtshungs dang tog dkar po / /
byang chub sems ma hA ba la /
dpa' legs gsung ba / /
gnyis med pa dang rtsod pa bral / /
sku gsum yon tan 'byung gnas dang / /
dri ma mi mnga' byams chen ldan / /
byang chub pa dang sa bcur son / /
thams cad rtogs dang dgra las rgyal /
72 /
shAkya seng ge gau tam / /
zas gtsang sras dang shAkya thub / /
rdo rje gdan pa sa 'tsho'i bdag /
don kun grub pa don grub dang / /
bla ma lha mo sgyu 'phrul sras / /
lhas byin rnams dang sgyu 'phrul sras / /
nyi ma'i rigs 'khrungs nyi ma'i gnyen / /
don thams ston pa thub pa la mtshan bcu drug /
cad pa dge sbyong che /
16 /
'di yi longs spyod rdzogs bstan sras / /
grags 'dzin skyes dang sgra gcan 'dzin /
1 /

3 /

6 /
nyan thos slob ma'i ming can no / /
byams pa la mtshan bzhi /

de bzhin sangs rgyas mi pham pa / /
'jig rten dbang phyug chu skyes can / /

'jig rten mgon dang spyan ras gzigs / /
rdo rje nyi ma brtson 'grus che / /
'jig rten dbang dang pad+mas mtshan / /
bdud rtsi'i char ldan yid bzhin nor / /
gzugs spyan ras gzigs la mtshan nyer gsum /
mang ha la ha la dang / /
bde ldan dbang phyug bu mo dgyes / /
'od dpag med pa'i thod can dang / /
za ma tog bkod mnar med gzigs / /
gru 'dzin ri la dgyes pa dang / /
yon tan rin chen 'byung gnas so /
13 /
sgrol ma sgrol ma zhi ba dang / /

yangs pa can ma sgrol ma che / /

dbyangs can ma'o /
18 /

2 /

3 /
'od zer can ma zhal gsum ma / /

24 /

6 /
